### Find Leads
Get a verified list of 700M+ contacts and 60M+ companies to perform outreach at scale.
  * ![AI Lead Finder](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-lead-finder-find-black.svg) ![AI Lead Finder](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-lead-finder-find.svg) AI Lead Finder
Just type what you need, right from the job title to company size, and AI will find the prospect details for you both accurately and instantly.
![AI Lead Finder](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/1-lead-finder-ai-lead-finder-image.webp)
  * ![People & Company Tab](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/people-company-black.svg) ![People & Company Tab](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/people-company-blue.svg) People & Company Tab
Switch between dedicated People and Company tabs, each with independent filters and real-time results. Save those prospects straight into your Saleshandy CRM to keep everything organized.
![People & Company Tab](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/2-lead-finder-people-and-company-tab-image.webp)
  * ![Advanced Filters](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-lead-finder-advance-black.svg) ![Advanced Filters](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-lead-finder-advance.svg) Advanced Filters
Use 70+ advanced filters across People and Company tabs, with 30+ rich data fields to build highly targeted prospect lists.
![Advanced Filters](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/3-lead-finder-advanced-filters-image.webp)
  * ![Waterfall Enrichment](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/waterfall-black-icon.svg) ![Waterfall Enrichment](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/waterfall-blue-icon.svg) Waterfall Enrichment
Fill missing data from multiple verified vendors and ensure every profile is fully enriched to the highest quality. Verify email addresses and import in one click.
![Waterfall Enrichment](https://www.saleshandy.com/sh2/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/4-lead-finder-waterfall-enrichment-image.webp)

Track prospects on visual Kanban boards with customizable stages. Update details, monitor activity, and close deals faster.

### Automate Outreach
Save hours of manual work by automating your hyper-personalized campaigns that run and reply on your behalf.
  * ![Prospect Search](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-ai-icon-black.svg) ![Find Search](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-ai.svg) AI Sequence Copilot
Let AI write, suggest, and modify your email sequences based on websites, ICP, and goals that make it look hyper-personalized.
![AI Sequence Copilot](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/AI-Sequence-Copilot.webp)
  * ![Data](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-flowup-black.svg) ![Data Manage](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-flowup.svg) Follow-up Sequences
Set up multi-stage follow-up sequences that respond to prospect behavior, whether they open, click, or ignore, to boost reply rates without manual effort.
![Follow-up Sequences](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Follow-up-Sequences.webp)
  * ![Multi-Channel Outreach](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-multi-black.svg) ![Multi-Channel Outreach](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/progress-analytic-multi.svg) Multi-Channel Outreach

What is Saleshandy? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Saleshandy is an all-in-one cold email outreach software that helps you find relevant prospects, personalize emails at scale, automate follow-ups, measure performance, and optimize your outreach.
It also has various AI-powered features like AI Lead Search, AI Sequence Generator, and AI Enrichment to make you and your team more efficient at booking more meetings and closing more deals with less effort.
What makes Saleshandy different from other tools? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Saleshandy stands out from other tools in the market because it offers all the outreach functionalities under a single platform. Be it prospecting, deliverability setup, or full-fledged outreach, users can run everything without paying any hefty charges.
• Saleshandy offers the biggest database of 700M+ contacts with one-click import to add selected prospect emails into the sequence.  
• Saleshandy offers unlimited email accounts without any extra charges.  
• Users can add unlimited clients and team members to make their outreach more successful.  
• Additionally, Saleshandy offers AI Sequence Copilot, AI Variant, and AI Lead Finder capabilities to make outreach more meaningful and personalized. 
From where can I get the Saleshandy demo? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
You can book a live demo directly from the Saleshandy Demo Page or contact the sales team at sales@saleshandy.com.
Does Saleshandy offer a free sign-up? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Yes, Saleshandy offers a 7-day free trial with access to all the major features.
Is Saleshandy suitable for both small and large-scale businesses? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Yes. Saleshandy is suited for businesses and lead generation agencies of all sizes, as it is highly scalable and cost-effective.
With Saleshandy, you get unlimited email accounts to scale outreach, the ability to invite as many team members as you want to collaborate and manage campaigns, and the option to add and manage unlimited clients. All of this comes without any extra charges.
Do I get verified contact data with Saleshandy? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Yes. Saleshandy verifies every prospect’s email address before revealing it to you. If the email address is invalid or becomes invalid later, your credit will be automatically refunded.
How can I reach the Saleshandy team? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
You can connect with the team via email:
• For sales enquiries: sales@saleshandy.com  
• For support: support@saleshandy.com  
• For marketing, partnerships, and collaborations: contribute@saleshandy.com
What native integrations does Saleshandy offer? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Saleshandy offers native integrations with CRM tools such as Pipedrive, HubSpot, Salesforce, and Zoho CRM. It also connects with email deliverability tools like TrulyInbox and email service providers such as Google and Microsoft.
Can I integrate Saleshandy with my existing tools? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Yes. You can easily integrate Saleshandy with your existing tools. You can check the integrations section to see all supported apps. If the platform you use is not listed, you can use Saleshandy’s API or Zapier to create custom integrations that work for you.
Can Saleshandy write my emails? ![Plus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/plus_acc.svg) ![Minus](https://www.saleshandy.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/minus_acc.svg)
Yes, you can use Saleshandy’s AI Sequence Copilot to generate highly personalized cold email sequences tailored to your business goals, offers, and target audience.

# Create. Convert. Close.
Salesloft gives you a complete picture of your revenue data to help:
  * Fill your sales pipeline faster with qualified buyers
  * Prioritize the right seller actions to win deals
  * Understand what deals are at risk
  * Drive more predictable revenue

### Revenue Orchestration Platform
#### Turn insights into action, all in one platform
Salesloft unifies AI chat agents, sales engagement, revenue intelligence, conversation intelligence, deal management, and forecasting — all supported by AI workflows and agents.
[Explore the Full Salesloft Platform](https://www.salesloft.com/take-a-tour)
### Analyze
#### Identify & repeat winning patterns
**Salesloft Analytics** centralizes reporting from across the buyer and customer lifecycle, providing visibility and comprehensive insights into sales performance to enable data-driven decisions.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/analytics)
### Chat
#### Turn website visitors into leads
**Drift AI chat agents** engage visitors with real-time personalized conversations, delivering a better buying experience and driving more qualified pipeline faster.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/drift)
### Prospect
#### Build pipeline & engage buyers
**Salesloft Cadence** takes the guesswork out of pipeline generation, lead nurture, and renewals. AI helps you prioritize the right buyers while providing valuable insights to improve every interaction.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/cadence-automation)
### Forecast
#### Call your number with confidence
**Salesloft Forecast** transforms your sales forecast into a strategic action plan to close more revenue by combining real-time deal data, AI, and your own insights to improve forecast accuracy.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/sales-forecasting-software)
### Coach
#### Uplevel your team's performance
**Salesloft Conversations** helps managers easily identify sales coaching opportunities and scale best practices with real-time data-driven AI insights based on seller activities, customer conversations, and deal status.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/conversations)
### Close
#### Accelerate sales opportunities
**Salesloft Deals** gives sellers the clarity and focus needed to win. AI insights help you understand where every deal stands, what’s at risk, and what needs to happen to speed up deal cycles and close more business.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/deals)
### Adaptive Experiences
#### Take the right actions at the right moments
**Salesloft Rhythm** turns buyer signals into seller action. Rhythm uses AI to prioritize the highest-value actions, helping sellers work smarter to win more deals.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/rhythm)
### AI Agents
#### Automate, optimize, and scale sales processes
**Salesloft AI Agents** work as an extension of your team, proactively handling tedious tasks, surfacing critical insights, and anticipating your next move.
[Learn More](https://www.salesloft.com/platform/ai-agents)
### The Salesloft Platform
#### Orchestrates and integrates at scale
Salesloft connects with your revenue tech ecosystem in one secure, compliant platform. This ensures your data is unified, your teams are aligned, and your decisions are backed by a holistic, enterprise-grade AI and data model.
[Take A Self-Guided Tour](https://www.salesloft.com/take-a-tour)

Three problems. One root cause: no account intelligence.

The Platform
## Research. Signals. Outreach. All on autopilot.
More pipeline. Less busywork. Every account. Every rep.
Deep account research
## 3 hours of research. Now 5 minutes.
Salesmotion consolidates executive changes, hiring signals, company initiatives, earnings analysis, and competitive moves into a single account brief. No more toggling between ZoomInfo, ChatGPT, investor relations pages, and news sites. One click, complete context.
Salesmotion is a no-brainer. It provides my reps with territory signaling capabilities that increase their effectiveness. They approach every prospect with ‘Why now?’ messaging.

Signal-based selling
## Capture every signal. Miss nothing.
Salesmotion monitors 1,000+ sources 24/7: news, earnings calls, SEC filings, job postings, leadership changes, funding rounds, M&A, podcasts, and more. Surface the signals and compelling events that matter for your business the moment they happen.
When outbounding, my team needs to provide the why. Salesmotion is invaluable for getting that at a fraction of the time. On top, it's not just for prospects but customers as well.

Smart prospecting
## Generate AI outreach that sounds like you did the work.
Salesmotion turns account research and buying signals into AI-drafted emails and LinkedIn messages that resonate. Every message is anchored to deep research — a strategic initiative, a leadership change, an earnings insight. Not a template. Review, refine, and send.
Saves me hours pulling together daily signals and internal briefings. It's a quick, easy way to bring teams up to speed and approach conversations with confidence.

## How Cytel’s commercial team cut research time by 50% and accelerated account planning
Cytel’s commercial team was losing hours every week researching accounts before meetings and planning outreach. With Salesmotion, they gave every rep instant access to account intelligence — reducing research time by half, accelerating account planning by 30%, and helping the team focus on selling instead of searching.
> “Salesmotion is helping Cytel elevate our enterprise sales performance by embedding account intelligence directly into our workflow. The platform gives our commercial team real-time visibility into key account movements.”

Why Salesmotion
## You didn’t trade manual research for manual prompting.
ChatGPT is great for one-off questions. But it can’t monitor your territory, alert you to buying signals, or scale across your team. Salesmotion can.
Factor | Salesmotion | ChatGPT / Manual  
---|---|---  
Account monitoring | 24/7 automated across your territory | Manual — one account at a time  
Signal alerts | Proactive alerts delivered to your inbox | None — you have to remember to check  
Research depth | 1,000+ sources, verified and cited | Training data only, risks hallucination  
Outbound generation | Signal-to-email in one click | Copy-paste prompts per account  
Time to insight | Seconds — always up to date | Minutes per prompt, stale data  
Team scalability | Entire team, shared intelligence | Individual prompts, no shared context  
CRM integration | Native Salesforce & HubSpot sync | None  
FAQ
## Frequently asked questions
Everything you need to know about Salesmotion
### Core product
What data sources does Salesmotion monitor?
Salesmotion tracks over 1,000 public sources in real time including company websites, news, press releases, earnings calls, SEC filings, job postings, leadership changes, funding rounds, and M&A activities to identify relevant account signals.
Is Salesmotion data always up to date?
Yes. The platform scans the web 24/7, ensuring signals reflect the freshest information available. Unlike ChatGPT, we're never limited by knowledge cutoffs — you always get current public web data.
What are account briefs?
Account briefs are AI-generated executive summaries of everything happening at a target account — from leadership changes and earnings highlights to hiring signals and strategic initiatives. They replace hours of manual research with a single, cited, ready-to-use document.
How does signal-based outbound work?
Salesmotion turns buying signals into personalized email drafts, call openers, and LinkedIn messages automatically. Each outreach message connects a specific signal to your product's value proposition so reps send relevant, timely messages — not generic templates.
### Getting started
How fast can I see value?
Users see buying signals and tailored account briefs within minutes of setup. Teams typically save hours weekly from day one and often book more meetings or close additional pipeline in their first month.
What does onboarding look like?
We load your target accounts, configure signal preferences to your ICP, and integrate with your CRM. Most teams are fully onboarded within a week. Your Customer Success Manager stays with you to ensure adoption.
Does Salesmotion work for private companies?
Yes. The platform can scan any company with a digital footprint, including private companies. It performs especially well tracking startups through podcasts, founder interviews, and job postings revealing growth areas.
How many accounts can I monitor?
There is no practical limit. Salesmotion is designed for territory-scale monitoring — whether you need to watch 50 strategic accounts or 5,000 across your team. The platform handles the volume automatically.
### Competitive / differentiation
How is Salesmotion different from ZoomInfo or Apollo?
Data vendors provide contact lists. Salesmotion delivers real-time, context-rich signals plus auto-generated account briefs and outbound drafts. We turn raw data into actionable intelligence your reps can use immediately.
Why use Salesmotion instead of ChatGPT?
ChatGPT cannot monitor accounts automatically, guarantee current accuracy, or scale across your territory. Salesmotion continuously monitors every account, auto-builds summaries backed by verified sources, and eliminates hallucination risks.
How is this different from my existing sales engagement platform?
Sales engagement platforms (Outreach, Salesloft) automate sequences. They don't generate the intelligence that makes those sequences effective. Salesmotion provides the research and signals that feed your engagement workflows with relevant, timely messaging.
Can Salesmotion replace multiple tools?
Yes. Cytel consolidated 5 separate research tools into Salesmotion. By combining signal monitoring, account research, and outbound generation in one platform, most teams eliminate subscriptions to 2–4 point solutions.
### Integration & security
Can Salesmotion integrate with my CRM?
Yes. Salesmotion integrates natively with Salesforce and HubSpot, pushing alerts and intelligence directly into your CRM. Our Salesforce integration is the most mature, with HubSpot close behind.
How does Salesmotion protect my data?
Your data is never shared or used for external AI training. Signals and research remain private to your organization, with encryption in transit and at rest, never accessed by third parties.
### Use cases
Which teams use Salesmotion?
Salesmotion is used by AEs, SDRs, account managers, sales leadership, and revenue operations. Any role that needs account context to sell more effectively benefits — from prospecting to renewals.
Can Salesmotion support account-based marketing (ABM)?
Absolutely. Marketing teams use Salesmotion signals to time campaigns, personalize ABM messaging, and prioritize target account lists based on real buying signals rather than static firmographics.
Still have questions? [Get in touch with our team](https://salesmotion.io/book-demo)

## Frequently asked questions
[How do I get started ? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Just add your LinkedIn account to SalesRobot!   
You'll be up and running in 2 mins.
[Is it safe to use SalesRobot? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Yes. SalesRobot uses residential IPs and mobile APIs, so your actions look completely natural. This makes it safer than tools like Expandi or Waalaxy, and our users have reported zero bans for months.
[Do I need LinkedIn Premium? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
No. SalesRobot works smoothly with a free LinkedIn account. Premium can give extra limits, but it is not required.
[What makes SalesRobot better than Expandi, Waalaxy, or Dripify? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
SalesRobot is safer, has stronger AI, and supports more channels. You get LinkedIn, email, voice notes, and a unified inbox, all in one place.
[Will my LinkedIn account get banned? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Very unlikely. SalesRobot uses mobile API behavior and real-time throttling to keep your activity natural and within safe limits.
[What can I expect from my trial? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Trials are meant to see the proof of functionality, which in our case means running a campaign. To get the best results, we recommend you spend 5 minutes to set up a campaign after you sign up. You'd be surprised how many people don't do this.
[What actions can I do using SalesRobot?  
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
You can like their most recent post, comment on it automatically, follow them, send them a connection request, automatically follow up with them and yeah, endorse their skills!
[How do I import prospects to SalesRobot? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
You can import people from LinkedIn Sales Nav search, a normal LinkedIn Search, or upload with a CSV, or you can DM LinkedIn group members or event attendees if you want!  
  
Did I mention that you can fetch all the people who commented on a particular LinkedIn post and request to connect with them?
[How does it work with LinkedIn limits? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
We fully comply with LinkedIn limits and you can send up to 75 connection requests a day. Additionally you can send up to 40 InMails a day to open profiles without using any InMail credits.
[How many LinkedIn accounts can I use ? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
If you've got multiple LinkedIn accounts you want to manage (client accounts for example), you can do that by just adding them like you added the first one.
[Can I use it with my CRM? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Yes! SalesRobot will populate your CRM automatically with leads interested in buying, directly from LinkedIn!
[Are all the features included in the trial?  
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Yes, of course.
[Can I send GIFs, documents in messages ? ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67dbe6c61ee3963a8ec4128b/67e50e0542da9f14c3d399f9_Sales%20Robot%20Website%20Redesign%20Accordion.avif)](https://www.salesrobot.co/)
Yes, you can send any type of attachment like PDFs etc.

FAQ
## Your questions, answered
[Still asking? Talk to a human.](https://seamless.ai/book-a-demo)
### What is Seamless.AI?
Seamless.AI is a real-time search engine that helps B2B companies find accurate sales leads so they can get in front of the right prospects, close more deals, and grow revenue at scale.
### How does Seamless.AI work?
Seamless.AI uses multiple data points that run on artificial intelligence to crawl through the web in real time and find, verify, and validate people’s contact information. Every time you search with Seamless.AI, our sales software scours the public web in real-time to pull the freshest, most up-to-date contact data for your sales list-building efforts.
### How much does Seamless.AI cost?
Seamless.AI is free for up to 50 credits. After that, we offer many pricing options to best fit your team's needs. [Contact our Sales team](https://seamless.ai/book-a-demo) to find a plan that fits your needs.
### Is Seamless.AI legit?
Yes, Seamless.AI is legit. We are the real deal. But don’t take our word for it.
LinkedIn ranked us at #7 on their 2022 list of the [Top 50 Startups](https://seamless.ai/customers/blog/marketing/seamless-ai-becomes-three-time-winner-of-linkedin-top-startups). G2 named us one of their [Top 100 Highest Satisfaction Software Products for 2022](https://seamless.ai/customers/blog/marketing/the-results-are-in-seamless-ai-is-a-2022-g2-winner). And we have amazing [testimonials](https://seamless.ai/customers/testimonials) of clients and [President’s Club winners](https://seamless.ai/customers/presidents-club/presidents-club-winners) we’ve helped generate millions of dollars in sales deals.
### What does Seamless.AI do?
Seamless.AI is a sales intelligence software that helps salespeople find the best leads.
Here are a few use cases:
  * You Need Sales Leads: You have a great product or service but need sales leads. Seamless.AI will help you identify your ideal prospect, figure out your total addressable market, and pull accurate contact information for those specific prospects.‍ 
  * You Have an Incomplete Sales List: You have a sales leads list, but it is missing information. Use our sales software to enrich your list and fill in missing contact information for your prospects.‍ 
  * You Have Companies You Want to Contact: You know which companies you want to contact but don’t have the contact information of the decision-makers. Use our sales software to find up-to-date contact information and build a quality sales leads list. Then email or call the prospect, qualify them, and close the deal! 


### How does Seamless.AI compare to ZoomInfo?
Seamless.AI is different from ZoomInfo because we are a real-time search engine, not a database. When you look up a prospect’s contact information on our platform, we search in real time to pull up-to-date and accurate information. By contrast, companies like ZoomInfo store information in databases that can quickly get stale and outdated. Our real-time searches, powered by artificial intelligence, are a defining feature that makes us different from anything else on the market.
### Is Seamless.AI safe as an add-on?
Yes, Seamless.AI is a safe add-on to your browser. You can also use our secure Chrome Extension as an add-on and turn your Chrome browser into the ultimate prospecting tool.

What is Seismic?
![](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/seismicsoftaff2-seismic6e3d-prod382f-e1b4/media/Project/Seismic/Motifs/accordion-line.svg?h=5&w=350)
Meet the **Seismic Enablement Cloud, the only unified AI-powered** revenue enablement platform that gives revenue leaders the confidence that their teams are ready to reach their goals – and the insights and tools to empower them to pivot quickly if they’re not.
[Explore the Seismic Enablement CloudTM](https://www.seismic.com/platform/enablement-cloud)
#### What can Seismic’s enablement software do for your team?
For revenue teams
Seismic gives revenue leaders the confidence to know their teams are ready to maximize every customer interaction — and provides the insights and tools to pivot quickly if they’re not. It drives productivity, scales best practices, and helps go-to-market teams [reduce costs](https://www.seismic.com/platform/reduce-costs) and [grow revenue](https://www.seismic.com/platform/drive-revenue).
[Learn More](https://www.seismic.com/solutions/teams/revenue/ "Learn More")
![Revenue Teams Screen](https://www.seismic.com/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fedge.sitecorecloud.io%2Fseismicsoftaff2-seismic6e3d-prod382f-e1b4%2Fmedia%2FProject%2FSeismic%2Fhomepage%2Fimage-homepage-for-revenue-teams-screen.webp%3Fh%3D912%26iar%3D0%26w%3D1216&w=3840&q=75&dpl=dpl_3MQrvNy5xKafQmnNUWoSikriHW1J)
For customer-facing teams
Seismic prepares customer-facing teams with the skills, content, tools, and insights they need to maximize every buyer interaction and [strengthen client relationships](https://www.seismic.com/platform/improve-customer-experience). With AI-driven insights and feedback to assess performance, managers identify winning behaviors, uncover skill gaps, and provide targeted coaching that drives continuous improvement for their go-to-market teams.
[Learn More](https://www.seismic.com/solutions/teams/sales/ "Learn More")
For enablement teams
Seismic provides enablement teams with a structured way to design enablement programs that drive your business’s strategic objectives. It empowers them to understand their impact, so field teams are ready, behavior change sticks, and every initiative drives measurable business outcomes.
[Learn More](https://www.seismic.com/solutions/teams/sales-enablement/ "Learn More")
For marketing teams
Seismic empowers marketers to influence buyer experience and pipeline growth by delivering the right content to customer-facing teams. With AI-powered automation and real-time insights, they can streamline personalization, refine messaging, and drive sales and marketing team alignment and impact at scale.
[Learn More](https://www.seismic.com/solutions/teams/marketing/ "Learn More")

## Sharpen your team’s skills by practicing with AI bots, not actual clients
### AI Roleplays
Can’t afford hours of live roleplays? Give your reps unlimited, realistic AI practice — tailored to your ICP and use case. Fully customizable for ANY call type & scalable across your team.
[Learn more](https://www.sellmethispen.ai/solution-for-sales-leaders)
![AI roleplays scenario preview and practice](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c0943868c0d17364c2d287_ai-roleplays.webp)
## **Show reps how to improve conversations and save deals**
![AI voice coach for sales reps](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c0962ca98bed85578e2e4a_AI%20coach.webp)
### 1:1 AI voice coach
Drowning in watching call recordings and dealing with delayed feedback? Give your reps an individual AI sales coach for every interaction — real client call or AI roleplay — and see their progress instantly. Fast, scalable, always on.
[Learn more](https://www.sellmethispen.ai/solution-for-sales-leaders)
## **Enable reps to learn by doing - right in their workflow**
### Real-time call assistant
Wondering why reps don’t apply their learnings? Give your team real-time AI support on live calls — so they never miss a key question or fumble an objection. Keep every rep sharp in the moment and driving better outcomes.
[Learn more](https://www.sellmethispen.ai/solution-for-sales-leaders)
![Real-time call assistant for sales reps](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c0979cdabe4c461bcecee8_AI%20real%20time.webp)

## Automate annoying admin tasks for everyone
[**AI customization**

### NO MORE UPFRONT HEAVY-LIFTING  

Customize your workspace in minutes by simply chatting with AI:  

  * **Create roleplay scenarios** based on your use case and actual calls.
  * **Build buyer personas** that mirror your actual prospects.
  * Design scorecards aligned with your sales methodology and framework.


![AI builder that creates roleplays, buyer personas, scorecards, and more in seconds.](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c09ec5511c78ef49981d0e_AI%20roleplay%20builder.webp)
### NO MORE LISTENING TO CALL RECORDINGS  

Get a reality check from thousands of conversations in seconds:  

  * **Monitor conversations at scale** to better understand client and rep behavior.
  * **Auto Q &A** to track compliance, playbook adoption, and performance gaps.
  * **Identify areas of improvement** for each team and individual.


![Analyze thousands client calls in seconds with AI insights](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c09ec545a41072d35db464_SMTP%20Insights.webp)
### NO MORE BACK-AND-FORTH ON WHAT TO PRACTICE NEXT   

Automate roleplay and coaching assignments:  

  * **Tailor exercises**
  * **Gamify the experienc** e through incentives and leaderboards for group assignments.
  * **Get notified** about everyone's progress.


![Assign AI roleplays and coaching sessions to your reps and track their improvement](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c09ec5e74ea11c32602969_Assignments%20SMTP.webp)
### NO MORE MANUAL NOTE-TAKING OR CRM UPDATE HEADACHES   

Reduce admin work so your reps can focus on conversations and winning deals:  

  * AI note-taking without adding another bot to the call.
  * Automatically update CRM notes for better data hygiene and smooth handoff to the post-sale team.
  * Generate AI-powered follow-up emails after each conversation.


![Let AI craft your follow up emails and automatically update your CRM](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/68c09ec5c073a190223e32a4_CRM%20updates.webp)

## Frequently asked questions  

### How customizable is SellMeThisPen for our use case and sales process?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
Fully customizable. Tailor scenarios, buyer personas, and objections so every practice feels like a real call. Build playbooks and scorecards around well-known frameworks or your own methodology, and customize the AI coach to follow your best practices at scale.
### Can we use the AI coach for both roleplays and real client calls?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
Yes. You can run coaching sessions with the AI after roleplays and after real client conversations. Reps get immediate feedback without waiting for a manager, and leaders free up time while still driving consistent coaching at scale.
### Is it only for sales teams, or can customer success use it too?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
It’s for both sales and post-sales teams. Any customer-facing team—from new business to customer success, account management, upsell, or cross-sell—can leverage it. Each team customizes scenarios and coaching to fit their unique use case.
### Can we request a custom integration?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
Yes. On our Enterprise plan, we build custom integrations tailored to your stack and workflow. You can [book a call](https://www.sellmethispen.ai/demo) with our team to explore requirements and timeline.
### What does onboarding look like, and how long does setup take?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
You can start right away with pre-built use cases, or use the AI roleplay builder to create custom scenarios in minutes. For larger rollouts, our implementation team partners with you to refine and improve over time—usually within 1–2 weeks. Most customers see meaningful value in their first 30 days.
### Do you offer a free trial or live demo?
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/649212eebf2446c71ee80c13/689d5ed013de9e574156fde7_689d588888053c9bafe42993_arrow-circle.svg)
Yes. Individuals can start a 7-day free trial of the Pro Plan by adding a credit card, though it’s limited to one seat and a smaller feature set. For business or enterprise plans, we recommend [booking a call](https://www.sellmethispen.ai/demo) with our team. That way, you’ll see the full platform in action, and we can discuss custom trials if needed.
Every great sales process starts with a great conversation.
Help your team build the confidence and skills they need to win with impact.

## Frequently Asked Questions
If you can't find an answer that you're looking for, feel free to contact us. Check out the [blog](https://in.sellifyai.com/knowledge-hub-and-resource-center) for more information.
What does Sellify AI actually do?
Sellify AI acts as a sales rep that initiates and manages real-time conversations with your leads via SMS. It qualifies prospects, overcomes objections, and books appointments — all automatically, so your team can focus on closing deals, not chasing them.
Which SMS platforms does Sellify AI support?
We currently support Twilio. If you're using a different SMS provider, let us know — we're actively collecting requests and may prioritize new integrations based on demand.
Can I customize how Sellify AI talks to my leads?
Absolutely. You can tailor conversation flows, objection handling, and brand-specific messaging to match the tone, policies, and sales strategy of your business. It's designed to sound like a real member of your team — not a generic chatbot.
How does Sellify AI know what to say?
We help you define your ideal sales flow — from first outreach to sale made. You can create instruction templates that guide how the AI handles common objections, explains your services, or responds in specific situations. You'll also have the ability to test these flows internally with your team before they go live, so everything feels dialed in and on-brand.
What kind of results and metrics can I expect?
Sellify AI gives you insight into conversion rates, reply rates, and overall lead engagement through a clear, easy-to-use analytics dashboard. You'll know exactly how it's performing — and where there's room to improve.
How long does it take to get set up?
Most customers are up and running in just a few days. If you're already using Twilio, setup is especially quick — and our team will guide you through the whole process.
What types of businesses use Sellify AI?
It's less about your industry and more about your tools. We currently integrate with CRMs like FieldRoutes, PestPac, ServiceTitan, and RealGreen, with more on the way. Don't see yours? Ask us — we can confirm what's available or add you to our CRM waitlist. You don't need a CRM to get started, though — we also support manual list uploads. Once a lead confirms they're ready to move forward, we hand them off to your team to close the deal.

General Questions
### **What is Smartlead's cold email outreach software?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Smartlead's cold email outreach tool helps businesses scale their outreach efforts seamlessly. With unlimited mailboxes, fully automated email warmup functionality, a multi-channel infrastructure, and a user-friendly unibox, it empowers users to manage their entire revenue cycle in one place. Whether you're looking to streamline cold email campaigns with automated email warmups, personalization fields, automated mailbox rotation, easy integrations, and spintax, improve productivity, or enhance scalability with subsequences based on lead’s intentions, automated replies, and full white-label experience, our cold email tool implifies it in a single solution.
### **What is Smartlead, and how can it enhance my cold email campaigns?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Smartlead is a robust cold emailing software designed to transform cold emails into reliable revenue streams. Trusted by over 31,000 businesses, Smartlead excels in email deliverability, lead generation, cold email automation, and sales outreach. A unified master inbox streamlines communication management, while built-in email verification reduces bounce rates.   
Additionally, Smartlead offers essential tools such as CNAME, SPF Checker, DMARC Checker, Email Verifier, Blacklist Check Tool, and Email Bounce Rate Calculator for optimizing email performance. 
### **How does Smartlead's unlimited mailboxes feature benefit me?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Our "unlimited mailboxes" feature allows you to expand your email communications without restrictions imposed by a mailbox limit. This means you won't be constrained by artificial caps on the number of mailboxes you can connect and use. This feature makes Smartlead the best cold email software and empowers you to reach a wider audience, engage with more potential customers, and manage diverse email campaigns effectively.
### **How does Smartlead, as a cold emailing tool, automate the cold email process?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Smartlead’s robust cold email API and automation infrastructure streamline outbound communication by transforming the campaign creation and management processes. It seamlessly integrates data across software systems using APIs and webhooks, adjusts settings, and leverages AI for personalised content.   
  
The cold emailing tool categorises lead intent, offers comprehensive email management with automated notifications, and integrates smoothly with CRMs like Zapier, Make, N8N, HubSpot, Salesforce, and Pipedrive. Smartlead supports scalable outreach by rapidly adding mailboxes and drip-feeding leads into active campaigns [Sign Up Now!](https://app.smartlead.ai/sign-up?utm_source=FAQ&utm_medium=Website&utm_campaign=Marketing&utm_content=Get%20Started%20For%20Free)
### **What do you mean by "unibox to handle your entire revenue cycle"?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
The "unibox" is one of the unique features of Smartlead cold email outreach tool, and it's a game-changer when it comes to managing your revenue cycle. The master inbox or the unibox consolidates all your outreach channels, responses, sales follow-ups, and conversions into one centralized, user-friendly mailbox.  
  
With the "unibox," you gain the ability to:  
1. **Focus on closing deals:** You can now say goodbye to the hassle of logging into multiple mailboxes to search for replies. The "unibox" streamlines your sales communication, allowing you to focus on what matters most—closing deals.  
‍  
2. **Centralized lead management:** All your leads are managed from one central location, simplifying lead tracking and response management. This ensures you take advantage of every opportunity and efficiently engage with your prospects.  
‍  
3. **Maintain context:** The "unibox" provides a 360-degree view of all your customer messages, allowing you to maintain context and deliver more personalized and effective responses.
### **How does Smartlead ensure my emails don't land in the spam folder?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Smartlead, the best cold email marketing tool, ensures your emails reach the intended recipients' primary inbox rather than the spam folder.   
‍  
Here's how it works:  
1. Our "unlimited warmups" feature is designed to build and maintain a healthy sending reputation for your cold email outreach. Instead of sending a large volume of emails all at once, which can trigger spam filters, we gradually ramp up your sending volume. This gradual approach, combined with positive email interactions, helps boost your email deliverability rates.  
‍  
2. We deploy high-deliverability IP servers specific to each campaign.   
‍  
3. The ‘Warmup’ feature replicates humanized email sending patterns, spintax, and smart replies.  
  
4. By establishing a positive sender reputation and gradually increasing the number of sent emails, Smartlead minimizes the risk of your emails being flagged as spam. This way, you can be confident that your messages will consistently land in the primary inbox, increasing the likelihood of engagement and successful communication with your recipients.
### **Can Smartlead help improve my email deliverability rates?**
![Email automation FAQs- Smartlead](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6204a703ff61516512c04f55/645de3477027d8b7408499de_faq_down_arw.svg)
Yes, our cold emailing software is designed to significantly improve your email deliverability rates. It enhances email deliverability through AI-powered email warmups across providers, unique IP rotating for each campaign, and dynamic ESP matching.   
Real-time AI learning refines strategies based on performance, optimizing deliverability without manual adjustments. Smartlead's advanced features and strategies are designed to improve email deliverability rates, making it a robust choice for enhancing cold email campaign success.

## Privacy Preference Center
When you visit any website, it may store or retrieve information on your browser, mostly in the form of cookies. This information might be about you, your preferences or your device and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to. The information does not usually directly identify you, but it can give you a more personalized web experience. Because we respect your right to privacy, you can choose not to allow some types of cookies. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings. However, blocking some types of cookies may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer.   
[More information](https://cookiepedia.co.uk/giving-consent-to-cookies)
Allow All
###  Manage Consent Preferences
#### Strictly Necessary Cookies
Always Active
These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.
#### Targeting Cookies
Always Active
These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.
#### Functional Cookies
Always Active
These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.
#### Performance Cookies
Always Active
These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.

# Built for modern commission management.
Spiff is a new class of commission software that combines the familiarity and ease-of-use of a spreadsheet with the power of automation at scale.
[Get a demo](https://spiff.com/demo/)
![](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/spiff-mobile-2.png)
![](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/spiff-banner-bg3.png)
![](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/chat-text.png)
![](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/chat-bubble.png)
## The leading commission management platform
Trust is at the center of Spiff’s cultural and technological DNA. We aim to bring that same trust to our customers’ organizations by introducing transparency, flexibility, ease-of-use, and real-time visibility into every step of the commission process.
  * ![Design](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/design-icon.svg) Design
Spiff Designer pairs the usability of a spreadsheet with the speed of automation to make comp plan creation a breeze. No matter how complex your team or goals, Spiff gives you the power to create the perfect plan in minutes not months.
[Learn more](https://spiff.com/platform/#design)
![Website-Image_Homepage-Design_May23](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/Website-Image_Homepage-Design_May23.png)
  * ![Motivate](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/motivate-icon.svg) Motivate
Spiff leverages the science behind motivation to help organizations foster happier, more motivated sales teams with easy-to-use features and functionality.
[Learn more](https://spiff.com/platform/#motivate)

## Solutions for every step of your commission process
Spiff has everything you need to manage commissions in one single platform. This streamlines workflows, enables easier communication, and instills a high level of trust across all stakeholders. With Spiff you’ll watch your commission programs thrive and your teams exceed their goals.
[![Finance](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/finance-image.png)](https://spiff.com/finance/)
## [Finance](https://spiff.com/finance/)
Stop spending hours building reports and rectifying a never-ending stream of commission errors. Spiff integrates with the tools you already use to ensure data accuracy and consistency.
[![Operations](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/ops-image.png)](https://spiff.com/sales-operations/)
## [Operations](https://spiff.com/sales-operations/)
Empower your teams and eliminate sales process headaches with Spiff. Our easy-to-use commission management software allows you to automate even the most complex commission plans.
[![Sales](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/sales-image.png)](https://spiff.com/sales/)
## [Sales](https://spiff.com/sales/)
Say hello to accurate, real-time commission data with Spiff. We increase visibility into the commission process and, as a result, improve trust, motivation, and job satisfaction within teams.
[![HR & Compensation](https://spiff.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/hr-comp-image2.png)](https://spiff.com/hr-sales-comp/)
## [HR & Compensation](https://spiff.com/hr-sales-comp/)
With Spiff, you can stop stressing about compliance, employee retention, or complex pay scales for commissioned employees. We help you automate the worst of the admin work so you can get back to your day.

# Scale Cold Email to Millions
Stop managing infrastructure. SuperSend handles the technical complexity of high-volume outbound so you can focus on your campaigns.
Book a Demo
![SuperSend dashboard mockups](https://supersend.io/images/featureshero_1.svg)
## Built For Scale
Sequencing + Enterprise Infrastructure for Millions of Cold Emails.
### The Problem
Most sequencers break when sending millions of cold emails. Deliverability fails. Campaigns don't execute.
### The Solution
SuperSend Relay — enterprise cold email infrastructure. Everything handled automatically. Built specifically for cold email.
### The Outcome
Send millions of cold emails reliably. Execute at enterprise scale without infrastructure management.
![SuperSend Relay Platform](https://supersend.io/images/Senders-screen---V2.svg)
SuperSend Relay
### SuperSend Relay Platform
Infrastructure built for 1M+ cold emails per month. We manage the IPs, subdomains, and deliverability so your team doesn't have to.
  * Fully managed enterprise infrastructure
  * Dedicated IP addresses & automated warmup
  * Subdomain rotation & reputation protection
  * Zero technical management required

[Learn About Relay Platform](https://supersend.io/features/deliverability)
![Sequencing Platform](https://supersend.io/images/Simple-Sequence-1---V1.svg)
Sequencing Platform
### Sequencing Platform
Orchestrate multi-channel journeys across Email, LinkedIn, and Twitter. Connect your own inboxes, use our provisioned mailboxes, or scale to millions with managed enterprise infrastructure.
  * Email + LinkedIn + Twitter sequences
  * Conditional routing & A/B testing
  * Connect your inboxes, provisioned mailboxes, or managed Relay
  * Orchestrate thousands of sending identities

[Explore Sequencing Platform](https://supersend.io/features/sequencing-platform)
![Super Inbox](https://supersend.io/images/inboxhome.svg)
Super Inbox
### Super Inbox
Maintain operational control over every response. Monitor and manage replies across thousands of senders from one unified view.
  * Unified Email + LinkedIn reply management
  * Automated response categorization
  * Real-time visibility across all senders
  * Centralized team workflow

[Learn About Super Inbox](https://supersend.io/features/super-inbox-automation)

How it works
## Symbo keeps it simple
![Sales Drive timeline silhouette](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bf90d11f4f187d6bb8b807_how-it-works-drives.svg)

### Engage
Drive prospects through series of steps to move the sales process forward, consisting of automated and manual emails, calls, video, social touches, and tasks.
![Sales pipeline silhouette](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bfe84104d33855bfc4359f_how-it-works-sales-pipeline%20\(1\).svg)
![Funnel silhouette](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bf921ec455c27dab34a14b_how-it-works-funnel-icon.svg)
### Pipeline
Plug the leaks in your pipeline and maintain sales velocity at scale by automating both next steps and record keeping.
![Drive campaign analytics graph silhouette](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/6196fa9bcf885cdccd719300_image-3-how-works-saas-x-template.svg)

### Improve
Optimize your sales team performance through A/B testing and metrics that track email effectiveness, call talk time, and sequence outcomes.

## Essential sales features
A single pane of glass for all of your prospecting activity.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bfe8aa1c5fbcd33735ca61_drives-icon.svg)
### Sequences
Multichannel engagement plans to connect with your prospects.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bfe9ee7fcc13878cb5c9fb_email-automation-icon%20\(2\).svg)
### Email Automation
Send personalized emails and automate follow up.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bfeb215662f7d20e93993c_analytics-icon.svg)
### Analytics
Track team performance and improve your outreach.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/61bfe9d78367b2cf97196f89_dialer-icon.svg)
### Dialer
Connect with prospects, record calls, and view call insights.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/6196fa9bcf885c7c68719183_icon-5-home-features-saas-x-template.svg)
### A/B Testing
Test email variations to compare reply rates.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6196fa9bcf885c039871912d/6196fa9bcf885cfa5f719181_icon-6-home-features-saas-x-template.svg)

DOMAIN SEARCH
EMAIL FINDER
EMAIL VERIFIER
The Domain Search provides a list of the people working in a company, with their name and email address, all found on the web. With 430+ million email addresses indexed, effective search filters, and deliverability checks, Tomba's email finder is its most powerful tool.
![Interface image](https://tomba.io/_ipx/f_webp&q_70&s_1000x766/assets/illustrations/home/search.png)
###  Find the right leads for you
Discover Your Ideal Prospects Leverage over 50 search filters to pinpoint contacts and organizations that align with your target customer profile.
###  Get their most important info
Acquire Essential Contact Details Secure your prospect's email and phone number. Gain insights into the technology they utilize, providing a valuable conversation starter.
###  Verify their data in real time
Real-Time Data Verification Tomba's instantaneous email verification guarantees that your connections are always with genuine, qualified leads.
###  Mobile Direct Dials
Access to Mobile and Direct Dial Numbers Obtain direct dial and mobile phone numbers for potential clients, facilitating seamless communication.

###  Business Finder

#  Unlock insights from F&I,Sales, BDC & Service conversations.
Meet the first AI conversation coach built for dealerships. Whether it's a face-to-face chat on the showroom floor, a service advisor in the bay, or a BDC call on the phone — our AI listens, guides, and helps your team capture more opportunities in real time.

## Deals Aren't Lost on Leads,They're Lost in the Conversation
### Reps freeze when it matters most
Traditional training doesn't prepare them for real objections. When pressure hits, they hesitate and the deal slips.
### Ramp-up takes too long
New reps spend months learning by trial and error. Without structured, repeatable practice, every customer call becomes an experiment.
### Managers can't coach at scale
Sales leaders are stretched thin. With AI roleplays and real-time alerts, every rep gets personalized, consistent coaching without burning manager hours and ridealongs.
## How It Works
Our AI conversation coach seamlessly integrates into your existing workflow, providing real-time insights and coaching across every customer interaction.

## Capture & Analyze Conversations at Scale
  * AI Call Recordings
Capture and review sales and service conversations across phone, web, or field with real-time AI-generated call insights.
  * Keyword Tracking
Monitor the usage (or absence) of high-impact phrases and messaging across calls to identify communication gaps instantly.
  * Conversation Scoring
Score rep performance based on custom rubrics aligned with your sales or service methodology.
  * Performance Analytics
Track metrics that matter. Spot patterns, coaching priorities, and rep-level trends over time with powerful dashboards.
